! This is a lexicon to be used with aspell spell checker only.
! Target is to use as many sublexicons as possible with as many variables 
! as possible to create aspell affix file.
LEXICON AspellAffix

!BISYLLABIC
! GOAHTI lexicon has consonant gradation and dipthtong simplification
! Cases: -i, -á, -u, -a, -e, and -o endings
! Obsolete because GOAHTI has same endings as GADDI ??
!buohkki GOAHTI ;
!buohkká GOAHTI ;
!duohkku GOAHTI ;
!fuohkka GOAHTI ;
!fuohkke GOAHTI ;
!buohkko GOAHTI ;
! GADDI lexicon has comparative forms
! Cases: -i, -á, -u, -a, -e, and -o endings
buohkki GADDI ;
cuohkká GADDI ;
duohkku GADDI ;
fuohkka GADDI ;
guohkke GADDI ;
huohkko GADDI ;
! IIJA non-gradating w/ a-ill
guohkkinymiija IIJA ; ! other case edings?
! STAHTA non-gradating w/ a/i-ill
buohkkistáhta STAHTA ;

!TRISYLLABIC
! SEAMU gradating trisyllabic
! Cases: -i, -a, and -u endings
jea0lu:jeallum2 SEAMU ;
kuo0mi:kuopmán2 SEAMU ;
muo0mu:muopmum2 SEAMU ;
nea0na:neatnag2 SEAMU ;
! MALIS gradating w/ consonant endings
! Cases: -is, -uš, and -ir endings
buoh0pis:buoh'pis MALIS ;
duoh0puš:duoh'puš MALIS ;
goah0pir:goah'pir MALIS ;
! GAHPIR non-gradating w/ consonant endings
! Cases: -is, -uš, and -ir endings
tuohpis GAHPIR ;
fuohpuš GAHPIR ;
foahpir GAHPIR ;

!CONTRACTED
! SUOLU contracted
! Cases: -u ending only?
suo00zu:suohccu SUOLU ;
! FALIS contracted
! Cases: -is only?
fálggis:fál'gis FALIS ;

!MISC
! LEXDIMINC diminutives
beanáš:beanáž LEXDIMINC ;

! Stray forms, with defect paradigms
sadji+N+Sg+Gen:saje K ; ! Normal is saji, this is hard-coded. 
hávvi+N+Sg+Gen:háve K ; ! Same here.
áigi+N+Sg+Gen:áigge K ; ! And here.
geassi+N+Sg+Gen:gease K ; ! Adverbial form, like those above.

eise#váldi+N+Pl+Gen:eiseváldiid K ; !SUB Wrong, but 18x in corp.
eise#váldi+N+Pl+Acc:eiseváldiid K ; !SUB
mátki+N+Pl+Gen:mátkiid K ; !SUB Wrong.
